============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK11)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A**c1 + c2*_m*sin(sqrt(A))
Candidate formulas: 53

GT is the fixed function (independent of \(t\)):
\[
f(A)= -0.8817392153705143\,A^2 + 0.5984688560365095\,\sin(\sqrt{A})
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) have no unavoidable \(t\)-dependence, (ii) produce exactly one polynomial term \(\propto A^2\) plus exactly \(\sin(\sqrt{A})\) with a constant coefficient, and (iii) have no extra nonzero terms (constants, \(A\), other nonlinearities) unless they can be set to 0.

Below, for each candidate I check whether its structure can be tuned to exactly \(-kA^2 + b\sin(\sqrt{A})\).

---

### 1. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3(A+c4)^{c5}\)
Can make \(Ac1\) and \(c2\) vanish (set \(c1=c2=0\)). But remaining extra term \(c3(A+c4)^{c5}\) cannot become \(\sin(\sqrt{A})\) for all \(A\). If set \(c3=0\), then no sine term. **No match.**

### 2. \(c0 + c1|A|^{c2} + c3|A|^{c4}/(c5+|A|^{c4})\)
Only algebraic/rational in \(|A|\); cannot produce \(\sin(\sqrt{A})\). **No match.**

### 3. \(A^{c0}c1 + A^{c2}c3\log(c4|A|+1)+c5\)
